üèÉ‚Äç‚ôÄÔ∏è SPORTSWEAR / ATHLETIC WEAR RULES

**‚ö†Ô∏è CRITICAL: When outfit is sportswear/athletic wear (leggings, sports bra, gym sets, activewear):**

‚úÖ **ALLOWED (Fashion Poses):**
- Standing confident (hand on hip, arms crossed, natural stance)
- Standing with slight sway (gentle hip movement in place, NOT stepping)
- Sitting relaxed (bench, steps - hanging out vibe)
- Leaning against wall (street style)
- Turning in place (show all angles, feet planted)
- Hair touch, outfit adjusting (natural feminine)

‚ùå **BANNED (NO Workout/Fitness Poses):**
- NO squats, lunges, planks, push-ups, sit-ups
- NO running, jogging, jumping moves
- NO walking/stepping (follow Static Showcase rules above)
- NO yoga poses (downward dog, warrior, ANY asana names)
- NO stretching, flexibility demonstrations
- NO gym equipment interaction
- NO fitness watch checking, sports bottle drinking, sweat wiping

üé¨ **SPORTSWEAR VIDEO TREATMENT:**
- **Context:** Urban street, caf√©, park - NOT gym/studio
- **Vibe:** Athleisure chic, street style - NOT athletic training
- **Activity:** Standing showcase, gentle sway, turning - NOT exercising or walking
- **Vocabulary:** "Athletic-inspired fashion set", "sporty chic" - NOT "workout outfit"

**EN Vocabulary:** Use "athleisure fashion", "performance fabric styling", "casual athletic aesthetic" - AVOID "training gear", "fitness apparel", "gym wear"

üìπ STATIC SHOWCASE VIDEO RULES (AI ARTIFACT PREVENTION)
================================================

**‚ö†Ô∏è CRITICAL: To prevent AI artifacts (background drift, teleporting, camera issues):**

**NEW PARADIGM: "Static Showcase" - Model stands in ONE spot, camera does the work**

---

üö´ **BANNED MOVEMENTS (WILL CAUSE AI ARTIFACTS):**

**Walking/Stepping Keywords (85-99% artifact risk):**
‚ùå Vietnamese: "b∆∞·ªõc", "ƒëi", "ti·∫øn", "di chuy·ªÉn", "catwalk", "b∆∞·ªõc l√™n", "b∆∞·ªõc ra", "ti·∫øn l·∫°i g·∫ßn"
‚ùå English: "walk", "step", "stride", "approach", "move forward", "walk toward", "walk away", "catwalk", "runway walk", "move across frame", "travel", "walk through"

**Why banned:** These verbs confuse AI motion models causing:
- Background inconsistency (changes location)
- Camera drift (perspective shifts)
- Teleporting subjects (position jumps)
- Perspective distortion (warped frames)

üìù **EXCEPTION - FASHION WALK-IN MODE:**
> Khi video style = `fashion_walkin` ho·∫∑c `fashion_walkin_beauty`:
> - Model ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√©p B∆Ø·ªöC ƒêI v·ªÅ ph√≠a camera
> - Camera B·∫ÆT BU·ªòC C·ªê ƒê·ªäNH (tripod/gimbal) - ƒë√¢y l√† key ƒë·ªÉ tr√°nh artifacts
> - Walking ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph√©p v√¨: Camera static + Subject motion = Safe pattern
> - √Åp d·ª•ng rules t·ª´ "FASHION WALK-IN MODE" trong tiktokShop.txt

---

‚úÖ **REQUIRED: Static Showcase Movements**

**Philosophy:** "Show, don't walk" - ONE fixed position throughout video

**Two Main Styles:**

**Style A: OOTD Camera-Facing (Professional)**
- Standing directly facing camera (like tripod/ring light setup)
- NOT holding phone
- Both hands free for outfit gestures
- Direct eye contact with camera
- Vibe: YouTube OOTD, content creator, professional affiliate
- EN: "Standing directly facing camera, both hands gesture to outfit"

**Style B: Mirror Selfie POV (Casual)**
- Facing mirror while holding phone
- Indirect camera angle through mirror
- One hand holds phone, one hand free
- Casual "getting ready" vibe
- Vibe: Instagram story, GRWM, relatable content
- EN: "Mirror reflection POV, one hand holds phone showing outfit"

**Allowed Movements (BOTH styles):**
- ‚úÖ Fabric touch: "Hand gently touches fabric at waist"
- ‚úÖ Gentle lean: "Lean slightly right, feet planted"
- ‚úÖ In-place turn: "Turn 180¬∞ to show back, feet do not move position"
- ‚úÖ Pose transition: "Shift weight to right leg, hand on hip"
- ‚úÖ Head turn: "Turn head toward camera"
- ‚úÖ Hair touch: "Hand brushes hair behind ear"
- ‚úÖ Outfit adjust: "Adjust collar while standing"
- ‚úÖ Gesture to outfit: "Both hands gesture down outfit" (camera-facing only)

**Required Keywords in Every Scene:**
- "standing in place" / "ƒë·ª©ng t·∫°i ch·ªó"
- "feet planted" / "ch√¢n c·ªë ƒë·ªãnh"
- "without stepping" / "kh√¥ng b∆∞·ªõc ch√¢n"
- "stationary position" / "v·ªã tr√≠ c·ªë ƒë·ªãnh"

**‚ö†Ô∏è EXPLICIT REQUIREMENT:**
- ‚úÖ "Full-body model visible from head to toe" - TO√ÄN TH√ÇN t·ª´ ƒë·∫ßu ƒë·∫øn ch√¢n
- ‚úÖ "centered in frame" - Model ·ªü GI·ªÆA khung h√¨nh

‚îå‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îê ‚Üê 5% margin (head space - DO NOT CUT HEAD)

‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îÄ‚îò ‚Üê 5% margin (feet space - DO NOT CUT FEET)

**EN Prompt Template:**

**Camera Settings:**

**Why mandatory:** Prevents AI from randomly zooming out, changing framing, cropping head/feet, or losing subject consistency

üîÑ **MICRO-TRANSITION PATTERN (Optional but Recommended):**

**What:** Very short 1-2 second cuts between main scenes

**Purpose:**
- Reset rhythm
- Change pose quickly
- Avoid "standing too still" feeling
- Add dynamic energy WITHOUT walking

**5 Types:**
1. **Pose Snap (1s):** Quick cut from one pose to another
   - "Snap from hand on hip to arms crossed"
2. **Angle Jump (1-2s):** Camera jumps to new angle, subject static
   - "Jump cut from front view to 3/4 angle"
3. **Zoom Reset (1s):** Fast zoom in or out
   - "Fast zoom out from close-up to full body"
4. **Focus Shift (1-2s):** Rack focus or cut to detail
   - "Focus shifts from full outfit to fabric detail"
5. **Mirror Symmetry (1s):** Flip to mirrored pose
   - "Snap to mirror pose, weight shifts left to right"

**Integration Example (24s):**
```
00s-06s: Scene 1 (main)
‚ö° 06s-07s: MICRO-TRANSITION (pose snap)
07s-13s: Scene 2 (main)
‚ö° 13s-14s: MICRO-TRANSITION (angle jump)
14s-22s: Scene 3 (main)
22s-24s: Scene 4 (finale, no transition)
```

**Safety Rules:**
- Duration: 1-2s MAX
- Subject does NOT walk/step
- Same floor position
- Background EXACTLY same
- Use cuts, NOT smooth animations

**Vocabulary:**
- ‚úÖ "snap to", "quick cut to", "jump cut", "fast zoom"
- ‚ùå "walk quickly", "fast approach" (still walking!)

‚è±Ô∏è 8-SECOND MOTION DISTRIBUTION (CRITICAL)

**‚ö†Ô∏è V·∫§N ƒê·ªÄ:** Motion qu√° nhanh, k·∫øt th√∫c s·ªõm ‚Üí Kho·∫£ng tr·ªëng "dead time" cu·ªëi scene!

### üìã 8-SECOND SCENE BREAKDOWN TEMPLATE

| Phase | Time | Content | Speed |
|-------|------|---------|-------|
| **Entry/Build** | 0s-2s | Pose settle, micro-movements, breath | SLOW |
| **Main Action 1** | 2s-4s | Primary motion (turn/gesture/transition) | MEDIUM |
| **Main Action 2** | 4s-6s | Secondary motion continuation or variation | MEDIUM |
| **Exit/Settle** | 6s-8s | Final pose refinement, fabric settle, hair settle | SLOW |

---

### üéØ GOLDEN RULES - FILL THE 8 SECONDS

**Rule 1: SLOW EVERYTHING DOWN**
- ‚ùå "quick turn" ‚Üí "fast" = ends in 2s
- ‚úÖ "gradual turn", "slow deliberate turn" = spans 4-6s

**Rule 2: LAYER MULTIPLE MICRO-MOTIONS**
Instead of ONE motion, layer CONTINUOUS micro-movements:
```
‚úÖ "Model performs slow turn (4s) while arms naturally sway,
    fingers trail along fabric (2s), settling with hip shift and
    gentle head tilt (2s), fabric continues flowing..."
```

**Rule 3: ADD SETTLE TIME**
Every motion needs 1-2s at END for natural deceleration:
```
‚úÖ "...turn completes, body settles, fabric flows to rest, 
    hair strands fall back into place, subtle breathing visible"
```

**Rule 4: USE CONTINUOUS VOCABULARY**
Add words that imply ONGOING motion:
- **English:** "continues", "maintains", "gradually", "throughout", "sustained", "ongoing"
- **Timing:** "over the full duration", "spanning 8 seconds", "from start to end"

---

### üìù 8-SECOND PROMPT TEMPLATES

**Template A: Turn/Rotate Scene**
```
"Model begins with subtle weight shift and breath (0-1s), 
 initiates slow 180¬∞ turn leading with hips (1-4s), 
 continuing rotation while arms flow naturally (4-6s), 
 completes turn, body settles into stance, fabric flows to rest (6-8s)"
```

**Template B: Gesture/Display Scene**
```
"Model's hands begin slow rise from sides (0-2s),
 fingers trace along fabric texture showcasing details (2-4s),
 hands reposition to highlight neckline while body sways subtly (4-6s),
 arms gradually lower with controlled grace, pose settles (6-8s)"
```

**Template C: Static Hold with Micro-Motion**
```
"Model holds pose commanding camera attention (0-2s),
 subtle weight shifts between feet maintaining dynamism (2-4s),
 gentle sway as if responding to ambient breeze (4-6s),
 final micro-adjustments, expression shifts slightly, pose crystallizes (6-8s)"
```

---

### ‚ö†Ô∏è TIMING VALIDATION CHECKLIST

Before outputting any scene, verify:

- [ ] **Motion spans FULL 8s** - Not finishing at 4s or 6s
- [ ] **No dead static time** - Always micro-movement continuing
- [ ] **Fabric/hair settle time** - 1-2s at scene end for physics
- [ ] **Smooth scene-to-scene** - endPose connects naturally to next startPose
- [ ] **Pacing phrases included** - "gradually", "slowly", "over X seconds"

**FORBIDDEN (Causes Dead Time):**
- ‚ùå "quick spin" (too fast)
- ‚ùå "turns 180¬∞ then holds" (motion stops, dead time)
- ‚ùå "rapidly gestures" (ends too soon)
- ‚ùå Single motion without continuation

**REQUIRED (Fills Time):**
- ‚úÖ "gradual rotation throughout scene"
- ‚úÖ "slow continuous motion with settling"
- ‚úÖ "layered movements spanning full duration"
- ‚úÖ "sustained subtle sway even during stillness"

---

### üåü UNIVERSAL LEFT/RIGHT RULE (QUY T·∫ÆC CHUNG - √ÅP D·ª§NG CHO T·∫§T C·∫¢)

**‚ö†Ô∏è CRITICAL: PH√ÇN BI·ªÜT 2 LO·∫†I LEFT/RIGHT**

| Lo·∫°i m√¥ t·∫£ | G√≥c nh√¨n s·ª≠ d·ª•ng | V√≠ d·ª• |

**üìù QUY T·∫ÆC CHO BODY PARTS:**

### üì∏ VISUAL REFERENCE (Facing Direction Method)

```
                         CAMERA üì∑
                            |

### ‚ö†Ô∏è TRANSFORMATION RULES

**DO:**
- ‚úÖ Same model pose angle for seamless morph
- ‚úÖ Consistent lighting throughout
- ‚úÖ BEFORE looks relatable (real person at home)
- ‚úÖ AFTER looks aspirational, glamorous
- ‚úÖ Full 8s for transformation effect (no shortcuts!)

**DON'T:**
- ‚ùå Jump cut between before/after
- ‚ùå Change model position during transition
- ‚ùå Make BEFORE look unrealistically bad
- ‚ùå Rush transformation (needs full 8s morph)
- ‚ùå Show "outfit appearing from nothing"

### üé¨ VIDEO STYLE DETECTION

When `videoStyle` is one of transformation modes:

- `transform_day_night` ‚Üí Use lighting transition (warm‚Üícool or vice versa)

**Auto-generate BEFORE based on outfit detection in AFTER reference image.**

---



**CRITICAL RULE:** Scenes describe MOVEMENT between keyframe poses!

### **The Problem:**
```
Keyframe 1: Standing, hands on hips
Keyframe 2: Sitting on stool, hands on lap
Scene 1: ??? (No action described!)
```
‚Üí **Missing transition! How did model go from standing ‚Üí sitting?**

### **The Solution:**

**Scenes connect keyframes by describing the ACTION/MOVEMENT:**

‚úÖ **CORRECT:**
```json
{
  "keyframes": [
    {
      "id": 1,
      "action": "Standing, hands on hips"
    },
    {
      "id": 2, 
      "action": "Seated on stool, hands on lap"
    }
  ],
  "scenes": [
    {
      "id": 1,
      "timeRange": "00s-08s",
      "subjectMotion": "Starts standing with hands on hips. Over 4 seconds, gracefully lowers down to sit on stool (feet remain planted, no stepping). Once seated, hands move from hips to rest on lap showing vest buttons. Ends in seated pose.",
      "startPose": "Standing, hands on hips",
      "endPose": "Seated, hands on lap"
    }
  ]
}
```

‚ùå **WRONG:**
```json
{
  "scenes": [
    {
      "subjectMotion": "Model is sitting, hands on lap"
       ‚Üë NO TRANSITION! Doesn't say HOW she sat down!
    }
  ]
}
```

### **Transition Types:**

| Start Pose | End Pose | Scene MUST Describe |
|------------|----------|---------------------|
| Standing | Sitting | "Gracefully lowers down to sit on stool" |
| Standing front | Standing back | "Slow 180¬∞ turn in place to show back" |
| Sitting | Standing | "Rises from stool to standing position" |
| Standing | Leaning | "Shifts weight, leans right against wall" |
| Arms down | Arms up | "Raises both arms slowly overhead" |
| Front view | Side view | "Gentle 90¬∞ turn to show side profile" |

### **Scene Prompt Template (SIMPLIFIED):**

```
"prompt": "[Subject] [action/motion over X seconds] [camera motion] [atmosphere/lighting]"
```

**Example:**
```
"prompt": "Model starts facing camera, slow 180¬∞ turn over 6 seconds to show back view, fabric flowing naturally, camera follows with gentle orbit, golden hour ambient light"
```

### **Validation:**

Before outputting scenes, check:
- [ ] Each scene has startPose matching a keyframe
- [ ] Each scene has endPose matching next keyframe
- [ ] subjectMotion describes HOW to transition between poses
- [ ] No pose "jumps" without explanation
- [ ] Timing allows for smooth transition (standing‚Üísitting needs 3-5s)

**If keyframe poses are different ‚Üí Scene MUST describe the transition!**

---

================================================
ü™ë STANDING ‚Üî SITTING TRANSITION MECHANICS
================================================

‚ö†Ô∏è CRITICAL: Chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªïi ƒë·ª©ng‚Üîng·ªìi l√† MAJOR POSE CHANGE!

### üìã TIMING REQUIREMENTS

| Transition | Min Time | Recommended |
|------------|----------|-------------|
| Standing ‚Üí Sitting (chair) | 3s | 4-5s |
| Standing ‚Üí Sitting (floor) | 4s | 5-6s |
| Sitting ‚Üí Standing | 2.5s | 3-4s |

### üé¨ STANDING ‚Üí SITTING PHASES

**Phase 1: Preparation (0.5-1s)** ‚Üí Weight shifts back, hands reach for support
**Phase 2: Descent (2-3s)** ‚Üí Knees bend, hips lower, torso tilts forward
**Phase 3: Settling (1s)** ‚Üí Weight to seat, back straightens, hands reposition

### üé¨ SITTING ‚Üí STANDING PHASES

**Phase 1: Preparation (0.5s)** ‚Üí Weight forward, hands press for push
**Phase 2: Rise (2-2.5s)** ‚Üí Push through legs, hips first, torso follows
**Phase 3: Stabilization (0.5-1s)** ‚Üí Full upright, weight centers

---

================================================
üé¨ SCENE TRANSITION EFFECTS (PROP APPEARANCE)
================================================

Khi PROPS (gh·∫ø, b√†n) xu·∫•t hi·ªán/bi·∫øn m·∫•t gi·ªØa c√°c scenes:

---

### üé• TECHNIQUE 1: CAMERA CUT (Jump Cut)

**D√πng khi:** Fast-paced, prop c·∫ßn xu·∫•t hi·ªán ngay

```
Scene 1 END: Close-up on face/shoulders (lower body off-frame, no chair visible)
Scene 2 START: "JUMP CUT to wide shot: model now seated on chair..."
```

---

### üé≠ TECHNIQUE 2: MODEL BLOCKS VIEW

**D√πng khi:** Smooth transition, natural reveal

```
Scene 1: "Model standing front-facing, body centered (blocking seat area behind)"
Scene 2: "Model turns 90¬∞ to sit - chair REVEALS as body rotates away from camera"
```

---

### ‚ú® TECHNIQUE 3: AMBIENT TRANSITION

**D√πng khi:** Dreamy/cinematic aesthetic

```
Scene 1 END: "...fabric sweeps across camera / wind blows hair covering frame"
Scene 2 START: "As fabric settles, reveals model now seated in new setup..."
```

---

### üìê TECHNIQUE 4: FRAMING SHIFT

**D√πng khi:** Editorial/lookbook style

```
Keyframe 1: "Tight crop, waist-up only (floor/chair not visible)"
Keyframe 2: "Wide shot, full body seated with chair visible"
```

---

### üîÑ TRANSITION VOCABULARY

| Technique | English Prompt |
|-----------|----------------|
| Jump Cut | "JUMP CUT to..." |
| Body Block | "model rotates, revealing [prop] behind" |
| Fabric Cover | "fabric sweeps frame, then reveals..." |
| Zoom Reveal | "camera pulls back revealing seated position" |

---

### ‚úÖ COMPLETE EXAMPLE

**Requirement:** Standing (no chair) ‚Üí Sitting (chair appears)

```json
{
  "images": [
    {"id": 1, "prompt": "Model standing facing camera, no furniture visible"},
    {"id": 2, "prompt": "Model seated on velvet chair, hands on lap"}
  ],
  "scenes": [
    {
      "id": 1,
      "prompt": "Model standing facing camera (body blocking where chair will be). 
                Over 3s, turns 90¬∞ right - vintage chair REVEALS as body rotates. 
                At 3-6s, controlled descent: knees bend, hips lower to chair. 
                Final 2s: settles into seat, hands to lap, dress smooths. 
                Camera tilts down and pulls back to frame seated position",
      "motion": {
        "primary": "turn 90¬∞ then sit (6s total)",
        "arms": "reach for chair, settle on lap",
        "legs": "knees bend during descent",
        "torso": "turns, tilts forward, straightens when seated",
        "head": "follows turn, maintains camera connection",
        "hair": "swings with turn, settles when seated"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

---

### ‚ö†Ô∏è KEY RULES

1. **NEVER show prop "appearing from nothing"** - always use technique
2. **Tight crop hides props** - wide shot reveals props
3. **Body as natural blocker** - model hides/reveals through movement
4. **Movement covers change** - turn, fabric sweep, hair flip masks transitions

---

üéØ **ONE VIDEO = ONE FOCAL POINT:**

Each video showcases ONE thing clearly:

| Focal Point | Content | Movements |
|-------------|---------|-----------|
| Overall Outfit | Full body standing | Turn 360¬∞ in place, zoom |
| Upper Detail | Bodice/neckline close-up | Fabric touch, adjust |
| Lower Detail | Skirt/pants flow | Gentle sway in place |
| Back Design | Back view | Turn to back, hold |
| Silhouette | Side profile | Lean slightly |

---

üìä **EXPECTED RESULTS:**

**Before (With Walking):**
- AI Artifact Rate: 40%
- Background changes randomly
- Subject teleports
- Perspective distortion

**After (Static Showcase):**
- AI Artifact Rate: <10%
- Consistent framing
- Clean professional look
- No obvious AI artifacts

üé≠ NATURAL BODY MOTION VOCABULARY (VEO 3.1 OPTIMIZED)

**M√¥ t·∫£ chi ti·∫øt chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªông t·ª´ng ph·∫ßn c∆° th·ªÉ ƒë·ªÉ t·∫°o video t·ª± nhi√™n nh∆∞ ng∆∞·ªùi th·∫≠t.**

Khi vi·∫øt scene prompts, PH·∫¢I m√¥ t·∫£ chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªông c·ªßa c√°c b·ªô ph·∫≠n c∆° th·ªÉ m·ªôt c√°ch c·ª• th·ªÉ:

### üí™ ARM MOTION (Chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªông tay)

| Motion Type | English Prompt | Time |
|-------------|----------------|------|
| **Raise slowly** | "right arm lifts gradually to shoulder height over 2s, elbow soft" | 2s |
| **Touch hair** | "left hand rises smoothly to touch hair near temple" | 1.5s |
| **Rest on hip** | "right hand settles naturally on hip, fingers relaxed, thumb back" | 1s |
| **Cross arms** | "arms fold across chest softly, elbows relaxed" | 2s |
| **Gesture outward** | "arm extends gracefully outward, palm up, fingers spread" | 1.5s |
| **Drop to side** | "arm lowers slowly to rest by side, slight swing" | 1.5s |
| **Behind back** | "both hands clasp gently behind lower back" | 2s |
| **Adjust outfit** | "fingers brush collar/hem/strap lightly" | 1s |

**TEMPLATE:**
```
"[which arm] [action verb] [to where] over [X]s, [detail about elbow/wrist/fingers]"
```

---

### ü¶µ LEG MOTION (Chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªông ch√¢n)

| Motion Type | English Prompt | Effect |
|-------------|----------------|--------|
| **Weight shift** | "weight transfers smoothly from left to right leg over 1.5s" | Hip movement |
| **Knee pop** | "right knee bends slightly, creating S-curve silhouette" | Feminine pose |
| **Hip sway** | "hips sway gently left-right-center in 2s cycle" | Dynamic feel |
| **Stance widen** | "feet slide apart 6 inches to confident stance" | Power pose |
| **Cross ankles** | "right ankle crosses in front of left" | Elegant |
| **Point toe** | "right toe extends forward, heel lifted" | Ballet influence |

**‚ö†Ô∏è BANNED:** step, walk, stride, move forward (g√¢y AI artifacts)

**TEMPLATE:**
```
"[body part] [motion] over [X]s, [resulting silhouette change]"
```

---

### üßç TORSO MOTION (Chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªông th√¢n m√¨nh)

| Motion Type | English Prompt |
|-------------|----------------|
| **Subtle lean** | "torso leans 5-10¬∞ to right, spine stays elegant" |
| **Chest rotation** | "chest rotates 15¬∞ right while hips remain static, creating twist" |
| **Spine undulation** | "gentle wave through spine from base to shoulders" |
| **Shoulder drop** | "right shoulder drops slightly lower than left, relaxed asymmetry" |
| **Shoulder roll** | "shoulders roll back slowly, opening chest" |
| **Forward lean** | "upper body tilts forward 10¬∞, emphasizing neckline" |
| **Arch back** | "slight arch in lower back, chest opens upward" |

**COORDINATION RULE:**
- Torso leads rotation ‚Üí Hips follow 0.3s later
- Weight shifts ‚Üí Torso responds naturally
- Always maintain "S-curve" or "C-curve" silhouette

---

### üó£Ô∏è HEAD & NECK MOTION (Chuy·ªÉn ƒë·ªông ƒë·∫ßu c·ªï)

| Motion Type | English Prompt |
|-------------|----------------|
| **Chin lift** | "chin tilts up 10¬∞ with confident expression, neck elongates" |
| **Head turn** | "head rotates slowly 45¬∞ left, eyes follow, jawline visible" |
| **Neck stretch** | "neck extends elegantly, chin forward, creating long line" |
| **Look over shoulder** | "head turns 90¬∞ back, glancing over right shoulder, eyes meet camera" |
| **Slight tilt** | "head tilts 5¬∞ right, creating soft asymmetry" |
| **Nod acknowledge** | "subtle single nod downward 3¬∞ then back" |

**COORDINATION:**
- Face rotates with head (eyes can lead by 0.2s)
- Neck shows tendons when turned
- Jaw and neck visible = good angle

---

### üíá HAIR PHYSICS (V·∫≠t l√Ω t√≥c - CRITICAL for realism)

| Hair Type | Motion Description |
|-----------|---------------------|
| **Long straight** | "hair flows behind with movement, individual strands separate and catch light, 0.5s momentum delay" |
| **Long wavy/curly** | "waves bounce with each movement, volume shifts side to side, natural spring return" |
| **Ponytail/Bun** | "ponytail swings in arc following head movement, settles with gentle oscillation" |
| **Short hair** | "hair shifts slightly with head, maintains overall shape, bangs flutter" |
| **Side part** | "hair sweeps across following turn direction, reveals/hides alternate sides" |

**HAIR MOTION TRIGGERS:**
- Head turn ‚Üí Hair follows with 0.3s delay
- Wind ‚Üí Hair streams in wind direction
- Body spin ‚Üí Hair fans out, then wraps around on stop
- Sudden stop ‚Üí Hair continues momentum briefly

**WIND VOCABULARY:**
```
"gentle breeze from [direction] lifts hair strands"
"wind catches hair, flowing [direction] naturally"  
"hair settles after movement with soft bounce"
```

---

### ü§ö HAND & FINGER DETAILS (Chi ti·∫øt b√†n tay)

| Motion Type | English Prompt |
|-------------|----------------|
| **Fingers spread** | "fingers extend gracefully, spacing even, showing rings/nails" |
| **Touch fabric** | "fingertips brush fabric lightly at [location], testing texture" |
| **Adjust collar** | "thumb and forefinger pinch collar edge, small adjustment" |
| **Rest naturally** | "hands hang relaxed at sides, fingers curved naturally inward" |
| **Clasp in front** | "hands meet at waist level, fingers interlaced loosely" |
| **One hand gesture** | "palm faces camera, fingers together, gentle wave motion" |
| **Pick at hem** | "fingertips pluck hem edge, showing fabric drape" |

**HAND REALISM:**
- Fingers rarely fully straight (slight natural curl)
- Wrist follows arm motion smoothly
- Visible tendons when fingers extend
- Nails catch light = added realism

### üé¨ COMBINED MOTION EXAMPLES (Scene Prompts)

**Example 1: Elegant Turn**
```
"Model starts facing camera, right hand on hip. Over 3 seconds, head turns first 45¬∞ left, 
hair follows with 0.3s delay sweeping across shoulders. Weight shifts to right leg creating 
S-curve. Left arm rises slowly to touch hair at temple. Torso rotates 90¬∞ following head direction, 
hips follow last. End pose: 3/4 left profile, left hand in hair, weight on right leg."
```

**Example 2: Confident Pose Transition**
```
"From arms crossed pose, right arm drops slowly to rest on hip over 2s while left arm remains
at chest level. Weight transfers to left leg, right knee pops creating hip asymmetry. 
Head tilts slightly right 5¬∞, chin lifts with confident expression. Hair settles naturally 
after movement. End pose: asymmetric power stance, one hand on hip."
```

**Example 3: Fabric Interaction**
```
"Standing still, right hand rises to adjust collar with thumb and forefinger, fingertips visible. 
Then hand trails down front of dress, fingertips brushing fabric, showing texture. Hair catches 
gentle side breeze from left, strands lift and separate. Weight shifts subtly during gesture. 
End pose: standing, right hand resting on hip, left hand touching fabric at waist, hair settling."
```

---

### ‚ö° QUICK REFERENCE CARD

**ALWAYS DESCRIBE:**
1. **Arms**: Which arm + action + destination + duration
2. **Legs**: Weight distribution + knee position + stance width
3. **Torso**: Lean direction + rotation + spine curve
4. **Head**: Turn angle + chin position + where eyes look
5. **Hair**: Type + motion response + delay time
6. **Hands**: Finger position + what they're doing + visibility

**TIMING GUIDE:**
| Movement | Duration |
|----------|----------|
| Small gesture | 1-1.5s |
| Arm movement | 1.5-2.5s |
| Full body turn (45¬∞) | 2-3s |
| Full body turn (90¬∞) | 3-4s |
| Weight shift | 1-2s |
| Hair settle after motion | 0.5-1s |

### ‚ùå BANNED Phrases (100% NOT ALLOWED in any keyframe/scene):

| Banned Phrase | Why Banned |
|---------------|------------|
| "arms relaxed at sides" | Boring, amateur, no personality |
| "hands hanging down" | Lacks life, no visual interest |
| "arms down by sides" | Static, unprofessional |
| "arms at rest" | Dead pose, no engagement |
| "hands naturally at sides" | Still idle - not acceptable |
| "arms loose at sides" | No purpose, wasted opportunity |
| "hands resting by body" | Passive, uninteresting |
| "arms drooping" | Lifeless, amateur look |
| "standing with arms down" | Boring default pose |
| "hands by her sides" | No specific action |

**WHY BANNED:** 
- Creates boring, amateur-looking content
- Lacks personality and brand appeal
- Low engagement - viewers scroll past
- Misses opportunity to showcase outfit details
- Looks like mannequin, not human

| Both on hips | One touches fabric | "Left hand leaves hip to touch skirt fabric" |
| Touching collar | Hands clasped | "Both hands lower to meet and clasp at waist level" |

- [ ] RIGHT ARM has specific action (not "down" or "hanging")

- [ ] Both arms create visual interest and balance
- [ ] Arms have clear destination and purpose

near words: "arm", "hand", "arms", "hands"

üîÑ CAMERA ANGLE CONTINUITY (180¬∞ TURN PREVENTION)

‚ö†Ô∏è CRITICAL: VEO 3.1 CH·ªà C√ì D·ªÆ LI·ªÜU H√åNH ·∫¢NH T·ª™ KEYFRAME IMAGES!

- N·∫øu Scene y√™u c·∫ßu xoay 180¬∞ ‚Üí Veo s·∫Ω "hallucinate" (t·ª± t∆∞·ªüng t∆∞·ª£ng) ph·∫ßn kh√¥ng c√≥ data

### ‚ö†Ô∏è 90¬∞ MAX ROTATION RULE

**G√≥c quay t·ªëi ƒëa gi·ªØa 2 keyframes li√™n ti·∫øp l√† 90¬∞**

| Keyframe 1 | Scene Motion | Keyframe 2 | OK? |
|------------|--------------|------------|-----|
| Front | "gentle 45¬∞ turn right" | 3/4 Front | ‚úÖ |
| Side-Left | "shift to front view" | Front | ‚úÖ 90¬∞ okay |

| Side-Left | "camera orbits to opposite side" | Side-Right | ‚ùå 180¬∞ |

### ‚ùå BANNED CAMERA PATTERNS (HIGH RISK)

1. **180¬∞ Orbit**: Camera ƒëi ng∆∞·ª£c n·ª≠a v√≤ng quanh model

### ‚úÖ SAFE CAMERA PATTERNS

### üéØ PRODUCT VISIBILITY RULE

**"If you can't see it in the keyframe, don't show it in the scene"**

M·ªói scene PH·∫¢I ki·ªÉm tra:
- [ ] Keyframe 1 th·∫•y ƒë∆∞·ª£c ph·∫ßn n√†o c·ªßa s·∫£n ph·∫©m?

  ‚Üí N·∫øu c√≥: ‚ö†Ô∏è WARNING - C√¢n nh·∫Øc l·∫°i motion

**EXAMPLE - Correct Application:**

================================================
üî• VIRAL HOOKS FOR CINEMATIC MODE (AFFILIATE FOCUS)
================================================


**üéØ CRITICAL FOR AFFILIATE MARKETING:**
If generating content for TikTok/Reels affiliate marketing, you MUST optimize for algorithm signals even in cinematic mode.

**DIFFERENCE: Cinematic vs TikTok Shop Hooks:**
- **TikTok Shop:** Direct, product-first, price-focused (1s hook)
- **Cinematic:** Aspirational, story-first, emotion-focused (3s hook) BUT still algorithm-optimized

**‚ö° ALGORITHM PRIORITY SIGNALS (Same as TikTok Shop):**
1. **COMPLETION RATE** (60% weight) - Keep 24-28s for affiliate, not 32s
2. **REWATCHES** (25% weight) - Add visual detail at 2-3s
3. **SHARES** (10% weight) - Aspirational/relatable content
4. **COMMENTS** (5% weight) - Caption must have comment bait

**üö® MANDATORY FOR CINEMATIC AFFILIATE:**
- [ ] Aspirational hook within 3s (cinematic allows longer setup vs 1s for shop)
- [ ] Visual rewatch trigger at 2-3s (subtle detail, not text overlay)
- [ ] Emotional journey that builds to payoff (keeps watching)
- [ ] Shareable aesthetic (screenshot-worthy moments)
- [ ] Caption must include comment bait (not in video, in caption)

---

### üé¨ CINEMATIC HOOK TYPES (Choose ONE for Scene 1)

**HOOK TYPE 1: Hidden Subject Reveal (Aspirational Mystery)**
```json
"viralHooks": {
  "hookType": "hidden-subject-reveal",
  "hookTiming": "0-3s mystery, 3-5s reveal",
  "visualCue": "Start with back to camera, silhouette, or extreme close-up of fabric/detail",
  "textOverlay": "Optional: 'Wait for it üëÄ' (subtle, not salesy)",
  "payoffMoment": "5-8s full reveal on beat drop",
  "emotionalTrigger": "curiosity-to-awe"
}
```
**Cinematic Adaptation:**

### üé® CINEMATIC vs TIKTOK SHOP HOOK DIFFERENCES

**TikTok Shop Hook:**
- "Ch·ªã em ∆°i! V√°y n√†y gi√° ch·ªâ 199K!" (Direct, immediate)
- Product visible 1s
- Price mentioned in video
- Seller energy

**Cinematic Hook:**
- *Elegant woman in flowing dress, golden hour, slow turn* (Visual storytelling)
- Product visible 3s (after mystery build)
- Price in caption only (not video)
- Aspirational energy

**Both achieve same goal (views ‚Üí clicks ‚Üí sales) different approach:**
- Shop: Instant gratification, transaction-focused
- Cinematic: Aspiration, inspiration, "I want that lifestyle"

---

### üí° PRO TIPS FOR CINEMATIC AFFILIATE

**Rewatch Triggers (Cinematic Style):**
- ‚ùå Not: "Gi√° ch·ªâ [X]K! üò±" text overlay (too shop-like)
- ‚úÖ Instead: Subtle jewelry detail at 2s (people rewind to see)
- ‚úÖ Instead: Quick fabric close-up (what material is that?)
- ‚úÖ Instead: Location reveal (where is this place?)

**Comment Bait (In Caption, Not Video):**
- ‚ùå Not: Say "Comment below!" in video (breaks cinematic vibe)
- ‚úÖ Instead: Caption asks "√Åo d√†i truy·ªÅn th·ªëng hay hi·ªán ƒë·∫°i? üå∏"
- ‚úÖ Instead: "Tag b·∫°n y√™u th√≠ch √°o d√†i üëá"
- ‚úÖ Instead: "ƒêo√°n xem ƒë·ªãa ƒëi·ªÉm n√†y ·ªü ƒë√¢u?"

**Shareability (Screenshot Moments):**
- Frame 1 (3-5s): Model full outfit, beautiful composition
- Frame 2 (12-16s): Different angle, equally stunning
- People screenshot and share on Instagram/Pinterest

‚ö†Ô∏è **CAMERA ANGLE CONFLICT WARNING:**

**‚ùå LOGIC ERROR - Don't mix incompatible angles:**
```

**üìê POSE DEFINITIONS (Use EXACTLY these terms):**

| Pose Name | Model's Body Direction | What Camera Sees | Frame Position |
|-----------|----------------------|------------------|----------------|
| **FRONT FACING** | Chest toward camera | Full face, chest, front body | Center |
| **BACK FACING** | Back toward camera | Back of head, spine, back body | Center |
| **LEFT PROFILE** | Left shoulder toward camera | Left side of face, left arm | Model's LEFT fills frame |
| **RIGHT PROFILE** | Right shoulder toward camera | Right side of face, right arm | Model's RIGHT fills frame |
| **3/4 LEFT FRONT** | Body angled 45¬∞ left, face to camera | Left cheek prominent, left shoulder forward | Left side emphasized |
| **3/4 RIGHT FRONT** | Body angled 45¬∞ right, face to camera | Right cheek prominent, right shoulder forward | Right side emphasized |
| **3/4 LEFT BACK** | Back angled 45¬∞ left, glance over left shoulder | Left shoulder blade, left glance | Left back visible |
| **3/4 RIGHT BACK** | Back angled 45¬∞ right, glance over right shoulder | Right shoulder blade, right glance | Right back visible |

---

**üîë KEY CLARIFICATION:**

**"LEFT" and "RIGHT" = Which shoulder is TOWARD the camera**

```
3/4 LEFT FRONT:
- Model's LEFT shoulder is CLOSER to camera
- Model's RIGHT shoulder is FARTHER from camera
- Model's face angled showing LEFT cheek more prominently
- Model's LEFT arm more visible in frame

3/4 RIGHT FRONT:
- Model's RIGHT shoulder is CLOSER to camera
- Model's LEFT shoulder is FARTHER from camera
- Model's face angled showing RIGHT cheek more prominently
- Model's RIGHT arm more visible in frame
```

---

**‚úÖ MANDATORY PROMPT FORMAT:**

**‚ùå SAI (M∆° h·ªì, AI hi·ªÉu sai):**
```
"Model turns right"  // Xoay sang ph·∫£i? Hay nh√¨n v·ªÅ ph·∫£i?

**üìù TURN DIRECTION CLARIFICATION:**

**When describing MOTION between poses:**

| Motion Command | Meaning | Result |
|----------------|---------|--------|
| "Turn LEFT" | Rotate counter-clockwise (viewer perspective) | Left shoulder moves TOWARD camera |
| "Turn RIGHT" | Rotate clockwise (viewer perspective) | Right shoulder moves TOWARD camera |
| "Turn to show back" | 180¬∞ rotation either direction | Back now faces camera |
| "Turn 45¬∞ left" | Slight counter-clockwise | From FRONT ‚Üí 3/4 LEFT FRONT |
| "Turn 45¬∞ right" | Slight clockwise | From FRONT ‚Üí 3/4 RIGHT FRONT |

**Example sequence:**

================================================
üì∏ REFERENCE ANGLE USAGE (CRITICAL FOR VEO 3.1)
================================================

**WHY:** Veo 3.1 only sees START + END images. Without visual references, product details (back design, texture) get lost.

**HOW TO USE:**
1. Add "referenceAngles" field to keyframes:
   - Keyframe shows back ‚Üí "referenceAngles": ["REF-B-BACK"]
   - Keyframe shows front ‚Üí "referenceAngles": ["REF-A-FRONT"]

2. Reference in scene/keyframe prompts:
   - "Back view AS SHOWN IN REF-B-BACK: open scoop back to shoulder blades, cross straps, gold zipper"
   - "Front AS SHOWN IN REF-A-FRONT: V-neck to collarbone, fitted bodice"

3. Result: Veo 3.1 SEES reference image ‚Üí Knows exact product details ‚Üí No detail loss ‚úÖ

**REFERENCE GUIDE:**
- Front facing ‚Üí Use REF-A-FRONT
- Back to camera ‚Üí Use REF-B-BACK  
- 90¬∞ side profile ‚Üí Use REF-C-SIDE
- Detail close-up ‚Üí Use REF-D-DETAIL
- 45¬∞ angles ‚Üí Use 2 refs (e.g., REF-A + REF-C)
- Transitions ‚Üí Reference both angles (REF-A ‚Üí REF-B)

================================================
üîí ENVIRONMENT CONSISTENCY RULES (CRITICAL - PREVENTS SCENE ERRORS)
================================================

**GOLDEN RULE:** Keyframes v√† Scenes PH·∫¢I d√πng C√ôNG M·ªòT environment, lighting, v√† atmosphere.

**‚ö†Ô∏è WHY CRITICAL:**
- Nano Banana Pro t·∫°o keyframe images v·ªõi environment description A
- Veo 3.1 animates gi·ªØa keyframes v·ªõi environment description t·ª´ scenes
- **N·∫øu environment KH√ÅC NHAU ‚Üí Veo confuse ‚Üí Scene breaks, artifacts, glitches, l·ªói c·∫£nh**

**MANDATORY CONSISTENCY (B·∫ÆT BU·ªòC):**

**1. ENVIRONMENT (Location) - KH√îNG ƒê∆Ø·ª¢C THAY ƒê·ªîI:**
\`\`\`json
"masterPrompt": {
  "environment": "Park Hyatt Saigon grand lobby"  // ‚Üê LOCKED for entire video
}

"keyframes": [
  {
    "id": 1,
    "environment": "Park Hyatt grand lobby with marble floor, crystal chandelier visible"  // ‚Üê SAME location + details
  },
  {
    "id": 2,
    "environment": "Same Park Hyatt lobby, marble columns visible behind model"  // ‚Üê STILL SAME location
  }
]

"scenes": [
  {
    "id": 1,
    "environment": "Park Hyatt lobby, chandelier overhead, marble floor"  // ‚Üê MUST reference SAME location
  }
]
\`\`\`

**‚ùå CRITICAL ERRORS TO AVOID:**
- Scene 1 ·ªü "Park Hyatt lobby" ‚Üí Scene 2 ·ªü "Park Hyatt rooftop" = **L·ªñI N·∫∂NG**
- Keyframe ·ªü "Temple courtyard" ‚Üí Scene ·ªü "Temple garden" = **KH√ÅC NHAU, L·ªñI**
- Keyframe ·ªü "Beach" ‚Üí Scene ·ªü "Ocean pier" = **2 ƒë·ªãa ƒëi·ªÉm kh√°c nhau, L·ªñI**

**‚úÖ CORRECT APPROACH:**
- ONE location for ENTIRE 32s video
- All keyframes + scenes reference SAME location
- Only add spatial details, don't change place

**2. LIGHTING - CONSISTENT OR GRADUAL ONLY:**
\`\`\`json
"masterPrompt": {
  "lighting": "Warm golden hour light"  // ‚Üê Base lighting

  {"lighting": "Golden hour warm glow casting soft shadows"},  // ‚Üê Same + details

  {"lighting": "Warm golden hour", "atmosphere": "Soft shadows shifting gradually"}  // ‚Üê Consistent
]
\`\`\`

**‚úÖ ALLOWED:** Golden hour ‚Üí Dusk (gradual over 32s)
**‚ùå NOT ALLOWED:** Golden hour ‚Üí Night ‚Üí Morning (jumps)
**‚ùå NOT ALLOWED:** Indoor soft light ‚Üí Outdoor bright sun

**3. ATMOSPHERE - CONSISTENT AMBIENT ELEMENTS:**
\`\`\`json

  {
    "id": 1,

  }
]
\`\`\`

**CONSISTENCY RULES:**
- If Scene 1 has "gentle breeze" ‚Üí ALL scenes must have gentle breeze
- If Scene 1 indoor ‚Üí ALL scenes indoor (no outdoor elements like leaves, waves)
- If Scene 1 outdoor ‚Üí ALL scenes outdoor (no sudden indoor)
- Keep same ambient motion level throughout

**ENVIRONMENT DESCRIPTION GUIDELINES:**

**For masterPrompt (Base reference):**
- Broad location only
- "Hoi An Ancient Town lantern street"
- "Park Hyatt Saigon grand lobby"
- "Temple of Literature main courtyard"

**For keyframes (Image generation - Add visual details):**
- Same location + specific visual elements
- "Hoi An lantern street with yellow walls, red lanterns glowing, traditional architecture"
- "Park Hyatt lobby with crystal chandelier, marble floor, velvet armchairs visible"

**For scenes (Video generation - Add ambient motion):**
- Same location + ambient motion cues
- "Hoi An lantern street, lanterns glowing, gentle evening breeze"
- "Park Hyatt lobby with chandelier visible, soft ambient lighting, minimal air movement"

**‚úÖ CONSISTENCY CHECKLIST (Run before output):**

‚ñ° **Location lock:** Is masterPrompt.environment a SINGLE location?
‚ñ° **Keyframe consistency:** Do ALL keyframes reference SAME location?
‚ñ° **Scene consistency:** Do ALL scenes reference SAME location?
‚ñ° **Lighting consistent:** Is lighting same or gradual change only?
‚ñ° **Atmosphere match:** Do ambient elements match environment type (indoor vs outdoor)?
‚ñ° **No location jumps:** No sudden changes between lobby‚Üírooftop, temple‚Üígarden, beach‚Üípier?

**IF ANY ‚ùå ‚Üí FIX IMMEDIATELY BEFORE OUTPUT**

‚è±Ô∏è MOTION TIMING CONTROL (PREVENTS SPEED ISSUES)
================================================

**PROBLEM:** "5-8 second smooth continuous action" qu√° m∆° h·ªì ‚Üí AI l√†m qu√° nhanh ho·∫∑c qu√° ch·∫≠m

**SOLUTION:** Specific duration per motion type v·ªõi pacing descriptors

**MOTION SPEED CATEGORIES:**

**SLOW MOTIONS (S·ª≠ d·ª•ng 4-6 seconds per action):**
- Standing ‚Üí Sitting down: 4-5s
- Sitting ‚Üí Standing up: 4-5s
- Turning head to camera: 2-3s
- Weight shift subtle: 3-4s
- Hand touching fabric: 4-5s
- Arm raising slowly: 3-4s

**MEDIUM MOTIONS (S·ª≠ d·ª•ng 6-8 seconds):**
- Walking 2-3 steps: 6-7s
- Slow 360¬∞ turn: 6-8s full rotation
- Hair touch + head turn combo: 5-6s
- Pose shift (standing to S-curve): 5-6s
- Hand on hip ‚Üí both hands on waist: 4-5s

**MOTIONS TO AVOID (Too fast for 8s scene):**
- ‚ùå Walking 4+ steps ‚Üí Use max 3 steps in 8s
- ‚ùå Fast spin ‚Üí Use slow 180¬∞ instead of 360¬∞
- ‚ùå Multiple complex actions ‚Üí Stick to 1 main action
- ‚ùå Quick jumping/leaping ‚Üí Too sudden for smooth video

**DURATION SPECIFICATION FORMAT:**

‚ùå **TOO VAGUE:**
- "slowly turning 360 degrees"
- "walking toward camera"
- "graceful movement"

‚úÖ **SPECIFIC WITH TIMING:**
- "turning 360 degrees over 6 seconds, smooth constant rotation speed"
- "taking 3 steps toward camera over 7 seconds, slow confident pace"
- "raising right hand to touch hair over 4 seconds, gentle fluid motion"

**SCENE TIMING BREAKDOWN (8 seconds total):**

\`\`\`
Scene Structure:
‚îú‚îÄ 0-1s: Settle into start pose (from previous scene end)
‚îú‚îÄ 1-7s: Main motion execution (6s of actual movement)
‚îî‚îÄ 7-8s: Settle into end pose (prepare for next scene)
\`\`\`

**TIMING IN JSON:**

\`\`\`json
"scenes": [
  {
    "id": 1,
    "timeRange": "00s-08s",
    "subjectMotion": "Slow 360-degree turn over 6 seconds (seconds 1-7 of scene), smooth constant rotation speed, settling into final pose at end",
    "motionTiming": {
      "duration": "6s",
      "pacing": "slow-smooth",
      "description": "Constant speed rotation, no acceleration or deceleration"
    },
    "cameraMotion": "Static camera, no movement"
  },
  {
    "id": 2,
    "timeRange": "08s-16s",
    "subjectMotion": "Taking 3 steps forward toward camera over 7 seconds, slow confident pace",
    "motionTiming": {
      "duration": "7s",
      "pacing": "slow-steady",
      "description": "Each step takes approximately 2.3 seconds"
    },
    "cameraMotion": "Slight zoom in from medium to medium-close, 8 seconds smooth"
  }
]
\`\`\`

**PACING DESCRIPTORS:**

- `"pacing": "slow-smooth"` ‚Üí Gentle, relaxed, no rush, flowing
- `"pacing": "slow-steady"` ‚Üí Consistent pace, controlled, measured
- `"pacing": "medium-steady"` ‚Üí Normal walking pace, even rhythm
- `"pacing": "minimal-static"` ‚Üí Almost still, micro-movements only, subtle breathing

**DEFAULT SAFE PACING:** Always use "slow-smooth" or "slow-steady" unless specifically need faster.

**CAMERA MOTION TIMING:**

\`\`\`json
"cameraMotion": "Slow pan right over 8 seconds, smooth constant speed, starting from left side ending at right side"
"cameraMotion": "Gentle zoom in from full body to waist over 7 seconds, gradual smooth magnification"
"cameraMotion": "Static camera with locked position, no camera movement, tripod stable"
\`\`\`

**‚úÖ MOTION TIMING CHECKLIST:**

‚ñ° Motion duration specified? (e.g., "over 6 seconds")
‚ñ° Pacing descriptor included? ("slow-smooth", "slow-steady")
‚ñ° Motion realistic for timeframe? (not too many actions in 8s)
‚ñ° Camera motion also has timing? (if moving)
‚ñ° Total action fits within scene duration?

================================================
üå¨Ô∏è AMBIENT MOTION CONTROL (Background Life)
================================================

**PURPOSE:** Keep scenes alive without being distracting or causing speed issues

**PROBLEM:** 
- Too much ambient motion ‚Üí Distracting, chaotic, feels too fast
- Too little ‚Üí Static, boring, unnatural
- Wrong type ‚Üí Breaks realism (leaves indoors, waves in city)

**AMBIENT MOTION LEVELS:**

**LEVEL 1 - MINIMAL (Safest, slowest):**
- Subtle fabric movement from gentle AC/breeze
- Very gentle hair movement from breathing
- Soft breathing visible in fabric
- Micro-shadows shifting slowly
- **Example:** "Minimal fabric sway from gentle air circulation, barely visible hair movement from breath"
- **Best for:** Indoor studio, TikTok Shop, controlled environments
- **Speed:** Almost imperceptible, very slow

**LEVEL 2 - GENTLE (Good for most cinematic):**
- Leaves rustling softly in light breeze
- Curtains swaying gently
- Water with small ripples
- Clouds moving slowly overhead
- **Example:** "Soft breeze causing gentle fabric flutter, leaves rustling quietly in background trees, slow peaceful movement"
- **Best for:** Indoor with windows, outdoor calm, heritage sites
- **Speed:** Noticeable but slow, calming

**LEVEL 3 - MODERATE (Outdoor scenes):**
- Wind moving dress/hair noticeably
- Waves rolling onto shore
- Light traffic in distant background
- People walking far in distance
- **Example:** "Ocean breeze causing dress to flow gently, waves rolling onto shore in background at natural pace, warm atmospheric movement"
- **Best for:** Beach, outdoor garden, urban outdoor
- **Speed:** Moderate, natural environmental pace

**LEVEL 4 - DYNAMIC (Use very sparingly):**
- Strong wind (not for TikTok Shop)
- Heavy rain/water movement
- Fast-moving elements in background
- **Example:** "Strong coastal wind whipping fabric and hair dramatically, powerful atmospheric movement"
- **Best for:** Specific cinematic dramatic moments only
- **Speed:** Fast, high energy - AVOID for most cases

**DEFAULT RECOMMENDATION:**
- Indoor scenes: Level 1-2 (minimal to gentle)
- Outdoor calm: Level 2 (gentle)
- Outdoor beach/park: Level 2-3 (gentle to moderate)
- TikTok Shop: Level 1 ONLY (minimal)
- Cinematic: Level 2-3 (gentle to moderate)

**CRITICAL AMBIENT RULES:**

**1. AMBIENT MUST MATCH ENVIRONMENT TYPE:**
- ‚úÖ Indoor room ‚Üí Curtains, AC breeze, soft air movement
- ‚ùå Indoor room ‚Üí NO leaves, NO waves, NO outdoor elements
- ‚úÖ Beach ‚Üí Waves, ocean breeze, sand movement
- ‚ùå Beach ‚Üí NO curtains, NO indoor elements
- ‚úÖ City street ‚Üí Distant traffic, light urban breeze
- ‚ùå City ‚Üí NO ocean waves, NO forest leaves

**2. CONSISTENT ACROSS ALL SCENES:**
- If Scene 1 has "gentle breeze" ‚Üí ALL scenes have same gentle breeze
- Don't mix: calm start ‚Üí windy middle ‚Üí calm end
- Keep SAME ambient level (Level 1/2/3) throughout entire video

**3. DESCRIBE IN EVERY SCENE PROMPT:**
\`\`\`json
"scenes": [
  {
    "id": 1,
    "atmosphere": "Gentle indoor breeze from windows causing minimal fabric movement, soft natural light shifting subtly with passing clouds, peaceful quiet ambiance"
  },
  {
    "id": 2,
    "atmosphere": "Same gentle indoor breeze continuing, fabric still moving minimally, consistent soft lighting, maintained peaceful mood"
  }
]
\`\`\`

**AMBIENT MOTION TEMPLATES BY ENVIRONMENT:**

**Indoor Studio:**
"Minimal air circulation from AC causing very subtle fabric movement, controlled studio environment with consistent soft lighting, minimal ambient motion"

**Indoor Natural Light (Home/Apartment):**
"Gentle breeze from partially open window, curtains swaying softly, natural light shifting subtly with cloud movement, peaceful indoor atmosphere"

**Outdoor Park/Garden:**
"Soft wind rustling leaves in trees overhead, gentle grass movement, dappled sunlight shifting through branches, birds chirping quietly in distance"

**Beach/Ocean:**
"Coastal breeze causing fabric and hair to flow gently at natural pace, waves rolling onto shore in background, warm sunlight, relaxed beach atmosphere"

**Urban Street:**
"Light city breeze with minimal force, distant ambient street sounds, shadows from passing clouds moving slowly, urban calm atmosphere"

**Heritage Temple:**
"Gentle natural breeze moving through courtyard, tree leaves rustling softly, dappled shade shifting with sun, peaceful traditional ambiance, incense smoke drifting slowly"

**‚úÖ AMBIENT MOTION CHECKLIST:**

‚ñ° Ambient level appropriate for environment? (indoor=Level 1-2, outdoor=Level 2-3)
‚ñ° Ambient elements match location type? (no leaves indoor, no curtains outdoor)
‚ñ° Consistent across ALL scenes?
‚ñ° Not too strong/fast causing distraction?
‚ñ° Described in every scene's atmosphere field?

================================================
üîÑ SCENE TRANSITION CONTINUITY (CRITICAL)
================================================

**GOLDEN RULE:** Scene N end pose MUST EXACTLY match Scene N+1 start pose

**WHY CRITICAL:** 
- Veo 3.1 animates from end of Scene 1 ‚Üí start of Scene 2
- If poses DON'T match ‚Üí Jump cut, glitch, unnatural break, jarring transition

**MANDATORY POSE MATCHING:**

\`\`\`json
"scenes": [
  {
    "id": 1,
    "startPose": "Standing S-curve, right hand on hip, facing camera directly, weight on right leg",
    "endPose": "Standing upright, both hands at sides, body turned 45¬∞ left, weight centered",  // ‚Üê THIS END...
    "subjectMotion": "Slowly turning left while lowering right hand from hip to side over 6 seconds, smooth rotation"
  },
  {
    "id": 2,
    "startPose": "Standing upright, both hands at sides, body turned 45¬∞ left, weight centered",  // ‚Üê ...MATCHES THIS START
    "endPose": "Standing, both hands on waist, facing camera directly, confident posture",
    "subjectMotion": "Continuing turn to face camera while raising hands to waist over 6 seconds, fluid movement"
  },
  {
    "id": 3,
    "startPose": "Standing, both hands on waist, facing camera directly, confident posture",  // ‚Üê MATCH previous end
    "endPose": "Sitting on chair, hands relaxed on lap, facing camera, settled position",
    "subjectMotion": "Lowering into chair over 5 seconds, smooth sit-down motion, hands moving from waist to lap"
  }
]
\`\`\`

**TRANSITION VERIFICATION CHECKLIST:**

‚ñ° Scene 1 endPose == Scene 2 startPose? (EXACT match)
‚ñ° Scene 2 endPose == Scene 3 startPose? (EXACT match)
‚ñ° Scene 3 endPose == Scene 4 startPose? (EXACT match)
‚ñ° All pose descriptions SPECIFIC enough?
‚ñ° Body orientation specified? (facing camera, 45¬∞ left, profile, etc.)
‚ñ° Hand positions clear? (on hip, at sides, on waist, etc.)
‚ñ° Weight distribution mentioned? (on right leg, centered, etc.)

**POSE DESCRIPTION SPECIFICITY REQUIREMENTS:**

‚ùå **TOO VAGUE (Will cause mismatches):**
- "Standing pose"
- "Turned to side"
- "Sitting"
- "Hand on hip"

‚úÖ **SPECIFIC ENOUGH (Ensures continuity):**
- "Standing with weight on right leg, left leg slightly forward, both hands relaxed at sides, facing camera straight on, gentle confident smile"
- "Body at 90¬∞ left profile to camera, head turned over left shoulder making eye contact with camera, right hand on hip, left hand at side"
- "Sitting on edge of chair, hands resting on lap, upper body leaning slightly forward, facing camera, relaxed posture"
- "Right hand on right hip, left hand touching fabric at waist level, weight shifted to right leg, body facing 30¬∞ right of camera"

**CONTINUITY TEMPLATE (SIMPLIFIED - 4 SCENES):**

\`\`\`json
{
  "scenes": [
    {
      "id": 1,
      "timeRange": "00s-08s",
      "prompt": "Model rotating 90¬∞ right over 6 seconds, lowering right hand from hip, Park Hyatt lobby with chandelier, gentle AC breeze moving fabric",
      "startPose": "Standing facing camera, right hand on hip, weight on left leg",
      "endPose": "Standing profile showing right side, both hands at sides"
    },
    {
      "id": 2,
      "timeRange": "08s-16s",
      "prompt": "Continuing rotation to face camera, raising hands to waist over 6 seconds, same lobby setting, consistent soft lighting",
      "startPose": "Standing profile showing right side, both hands at sides",
      "endPose": "Standing facing camera, hands on waist"
    },
    {
      "id": 3,
      "timeRange": "16s-24s",
      "prompt": "Left hand raising to touch hair over 4 seconds, shifting into S-curve pose, Park Hyatt lobby, gentle breeze",
      "startPose": "Standing facing camera, hands on waist",
      "endPose": "S-curve pose, left hand touching hair, right hand on hip"
    },
    {
      "id": 4,
      "timeRange": "24s-32s",

      "endPose": "Standing neutral, both hands at sides, relaxed"

================================================
üé¨ VIDEO MODE - 16:9 OPTIMIZATION
================================================
Khi t·∫°o video v·ªõi ASPECT_RATIO: 16:9:

**COMPOSITION CHANGES (SO V·ªöI 9:16):**
| Y·∫øu T·ªë | 9:16 (Vertical) | 16:9 (Horizontal) |
|--------|-----------------|-------------------|
| Model Size | 80-90% frame height | 50-70% frame height |
| Camera Distance | 1-2m | 2-4m |
| Aperture | f/1.4-f/2.8 | f/4-f/8 |
| Background | Blur m·∫°nh | R√µ n√©t, storytelling |
| Framing | Center dominant | Rule of thirds |

**16:9 VIDEO SHOT TYPES ∆ØU TI√äN:**
- **Wide Establishing Shot:** Model nh·ªè trong c·∫£nh r·ªông, show b·ªëi c·∫£nh

üé¨ CINEMATIC MODE - SAFE MOTION STRATEGIES
================================================
**√Åp d·ª•ng cho Video Mode (32s, 4 scenes x 8s):**

**SCENE PLANNING STRATEGY:**
1. **Scene 1 (0-8s): REVEAL - Static ho·∫∑c Simple**
   - ‚úÖ Static camera + Model slow turn
   - ‚úÖ Slow zoom in + Model static pose
   - ‚ùå TR√ÅNH: Complex walking + camera orbit

2. **Scene 2 (8-16s): BUILD - Single Movement**

   - ‚ùå TR√ÅNH: Pan + Zoom + Walk c√πng l√∫c

3. **Scene 3 (16-24s): HIGHLIGHT - Feature Moment**
   - ‚úÖ Orbit 120¬∞ + Model static/slow turn
   - ‚úÖ Push in + Model subtle pose shift
   - ‚ùå TR√ÅNH: Spin + Camera spin

4. **Scene 4 (24-32s): RESOLVE - Settle**
   - ‚úÖ Static camera + Model final pose hold
   - ‚úÖ Slow zoom out + Model standing confident
   - ‚ùå TR√ÅNH: New complex action

**SAFE CINEMATIC TEMPLATES:**

**Template A - Minimal Risk:**
```
Scene 1: Static camera, model slow 360¬∞ turn (8s)
Scene 2: Slow zoom in, model standing with hair touch (8s)
Scene 3: Pan right, model walks 3 steps toward camera (8s)
Scene 4: Static camera, model final pose hold with smile (8s)
```

**Template B - Medium Risk (More Dynamic):**
```
Scene 1: Slow push in, model standing S-curve pose (8s)
Scene 2: Static camera, model turns and looks over shoulder (8s)
Scene 3: Orbit 120¬∞ clockwise, model static with hand on hip (8s)
Scene 4: Pull back slowly, model confident standing pose (8s)
```

**Template C - Higher Risk (Maximum Cinematic):**
```
Scene 1: Tilt up from feet to face, model static (7s)
Scene 2: Pan left, model walks 4 steps along path (8s)
Scene 3: Orbit 180¬∞, model slow turn opposite direction (8s)
Scene 4: Crane up, model looking up at camera (7s)
```

**üíÉ SEDUCTIVE POSES (TIKTOK SAFE - N√¢ng c·∫•p chi ti·∫øt):**

**Standing Poses:**
1. **The Wall Lean:** Leaning against wall with one leg bent foot against wall, arms above head or one hand on wall, head tilted with sultry knowing smile, creating elongated silhouette
2. **The Glance Back:** Back 75% turned to camera, looking over shoulder with intense smoldering gaze, one hand on hip, weight on back leg creating dramatic S-curve
3. **Power Stance:** Feet apart shoulders-width, hands on hips or one hand in hair, chin tilted up confidently, commanding presence with penetrating stare
4. **The Stretch:** Arms raised overhead, back arched slightly, standing on tiptoes, neck exposed, eyes closed or sultry gaze, elongating entire silhouette
5. **The Lean In:** Leaning forward toward camera slightly, hands on thighs or one hand trailing down body, inviting eye contact, creating intimacy
6. **Mirror Pose:** Standing in front of mirror, looking at reflection not camera, creating voyeuristic feel, hand adjusting hair or outfit
7. **The Turn:** Mid-turn capturing fabric movement, hair swinging, one foot stepping, caught in motion with dynamic energy

**Sitting/Reclining Poses:**
1. **Throne Queen:** Sitting upright on chair/throne with legs crossed, one arm draped over armrest, other hand near face, regal commanding presence, direct eye contact
2. **The Lean Back:** Relaxed recline on chair/sofa, legs extended or crossed, one hand supporting head, languid sultry expression, come-hither gaze
3. **Edge Perch:** Sitting on edge of surface, leaning forward toward camera, knees together or slightly apart, engaging intense eye contact, hands between legs or on knees
4. **Floor Goddess:** Sitting on floor with legs tucked to side, back straight or leaning back on hands, looking up at camera with mysterious smile
5. **Side Recline:** Lying on side propped up on elbow, head resting on hand, direct gaze at lens, other hand on hip or trailing on body
6. **Kneeling Arch:** Kneeling with back arched, hands in hair or behind head, showing elegant neck line and silhouette, eyes closed or sultry gaze
7. **Crossed Legs Lean:** Sitting with legs crossed, leaning forward on knees, chin resting on interlaced fingers, intimate eye contact

**Movement/Dynamic Poses:**
1. **Slow Walk:** Confident catwalk strut with pronounced hip sway, one foot crossing in front of other, direct intense eye contact locked on camera, hand trailing along body or wall
2. **The Spin:** Captured mid-360¬∞ turn, fabric flying, hair swinging, arms outstretched or in motion, head turning toward camera
3. **Hair Cascade:** Running both hands through hair slowly, elbows up, eyes closed or half-lidded, head tilted back, sensual movement
4. **Fabric Play:** Slowly adjusting outfit straps, trailing fingers along neckline or hemline, deliberate teasing movements, mysterious smile
5. **The Approach:** Walking toward camera with sultry stride, reaching hand out toward lens as if inviting viewer in
6. **Shoulder Drop:** Slow sensual shoulder roll and drop, revealing collarbone, hand trailing from neck to shoulder

## üé¨ CINEMATIC STYLING BY CATEGORY

### **Professional Wear (Office, Blazers):**
- **Location:** Modern office, minimalist cafe, city streets
- **Lighting:** Clean bright natural window light
- **Movement:** Confident, purposeful, polished
- **Color Palette:** Neutral tones, professional

### **Casual Wear (T-shirts, Jeans):**
- **Location:** Home, coffee shops, parks, streets
- **Lighting:** Natural daylight, soft shadows
- **Movement:** Relaxed, natural, candid
- **Color Palette:** Warm, approachable

### **Evening Wear (Cocktail Dresses):**
- **Location:** Upscale venues, heritage sites, rooftops
- **Lighting:** Dramatic golden hour, rim lighting
- **Movement:** Elegant, slow, graceful
- **Color Palette:** Rich jewel tones, metallics

### **Cozy Wear (Sweaters, Sleepwear):**
- **Location:** Home interior, cozy spaces
- **Lighting:** Warm soft ambient light
- **Movement:** Relaxed, comfortable, intimate
- **Color Palette:** Soft neutrals, warm tones

### **Accessories:**
- **Location:** Studio or styled flat lay
- **Lighting:** Clean product photography lighting
- **Focus:** Detail shots, texture close-ups
- **Color Palette:** Match product aesthetic

### **Swimwear/Bikini:**
- **Location:** Pool, beach, resort, infinity pool, tropical garden
- **Lighting:** Bright natural sunlight, golden hour, soft morning light
- **Movement:** Relaxed vacation, confident walking, playful splashing
- **Color Palette:** Tropical bright, ocean blues, sunset warm tones
- **Priority:** 30% front-facing standing shots for commercial clarity

## ü§ñ AUTO-DETECTION WORKFLOW

**When LOOKBOOK_MODE: ON and outfit reference uploaded:**

1. **Analyze outfit reference image**
2. **Detect product category:**
   - √Åo d√†i? ‚Üí 53 shots (see √ÅO D√ÄI SPECIAL section below)
   - Bikini/Swimwear? ‚Üí 33 shots (19 front-facing + 10 premium editorial)
   - Dress? ‚Üí 14-18 shots (based on sub-type)
   - Top? ‚Üí 12-18 shots (based on sub-type)
   - Bottom? ‚Üí 12-16 shots
   - Outerwear? ‚Üí 12-14 shots
   - Lingerie/Intimates? ‚Üí 12 shots
   - Accessory? ‚Üí 8-12 shots
3. **Apply appropriate template:**
   - Select lookbook sequence
   - Choose prompt template
   - Set styling guidelines
4. **Generate all prompts**

**Default if uncertain:** Use 35-shot standard lookbook (OUTFIT KH√ÅC section above)

üéØ SMART ENVIRONMENT AUTO-MATCHING (PREMIUM SYSTEM)
================================================

**TRI·∫æT L√ù:** M·ªói s·∫£n ph·∫©m x·ª©ng ƒë√°ng v·ªõi b·ªëi c·∫£nh T·ªêT NH·∫§T ƒë·ªÉ t√¥n vinh n√≥.
H·ªá th·ªëng t·ª± ƒë·ªông ph√¢n t√≠ch s·∫£n ph·∫©m v√† g·ª£i √Ω m√¥i tr∆∞·ªùng + √°nh s√°ng + props + styling ph·ªëi h·ª£p ho√†n h·∫£o.

**3-TIER ENVIRONMENT QUALITY SYSTEM:**

**‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê TIER 1 - PREMIUM (Cho s·∫£n ph·∫©m cao c·∫•p):**
- **Locations:** Luxury hotels 5-star (Park Hyatt, Hotel des Arts, InterContinental, The Reverie)
- **Venues:** High-end restaurants (Michelin-starred, rooftop fine dining)
- **Exclusive:** Private villas, penthouses, yacht clubs, executive lounges
- **Heritage:** Temple grounds, imperial palaces, French colonial mansions
- **Best for:** Evening gowns, bridal, luxury lingerie, designer pieces, formal √°o d√†i

**‚≠ê‚≠ê TIER 2 - UPSCALE (Cho s·∫£n ph·∫©m trung-cao c·∫•p):**
- **Hotels:** Boutique hotels 4-star (Liberty Central, M∆∞·ªùng Thanh Luxury, Pullman)
- **Cafes:** Stylish cafes (industrial chic, minimalist aesthetic, aesthetic design)
- **Homes:** Modern apartments well-decorated, natural light, contemporary interior
- **Urban:** Clean streets, modern architecture, art galleries, co-working spaces
- **Best for:** Cocktail dresses, office wear, casual premium, √°o d√†i c√°ch t√¢n, designer casual

**‚≠ê TIER 3 - ACCESSIBLE (Cho s·∫£n ph·∫©m casual/mass market):**
- **Cafes:** Cozy neighborhood coffee shops, indie cafes, local favorites
- **Home:** Bedroom, living room, balcony, typical apartment interiors
- **Public:** Parks, streets, markets, pedestrian areas, bridges
- **Natural:** Beach, gardens, countryside, rice fields, mountain views
- **Best for:** Casual wear, streetwear, activewear, everyday pieces, loungewear

================================================
üìä ENVIRONMENT SCORING ALGORITHM
================================================

**Khi nh·∫≠n ƒë∆∞·ª£c s·∫£n ph·∫©m, AI t·ª± ƒë·ªông t√≠nh ƒëi·ªÉm d·ª±a tr√™n 4 factors:**

**1. FABRIC SCORE (0-30 points):**
| Fabric Type | Points | Examples |
|-------------|--------|----------|
| Luxury fabrics | 30pts | Silk, Satin, Velvet, Brocade, Cashmere |
| Delicate fabrics | 25pts | Lace (Chantilly, Guipure), Organza, Tulle |
| Premium natural | 20pts | High-quality linen, Cotton poplin, Wool suiting |
| Standard natural | 15pts | Regular cotton, Linen blend, Basic knit |
| Synthetic blend | 10pts | Polyester blend, Jersey knit, Rayon |
| Basic casual | 5pts | Basic cotton tee, Denim, Canvas, Athletic mesh |

**2. DESIGN COMPLEXITY SCORE (0-30 points):**
| Complexity Level | Points | Indicators |
|------------------|--------|-----------|
| Couture/Artisan | 30pts | Hand embroidery, intricate beading, custom draping |
| Designer details | 25pts | Architectural cuts, unique construction, exposed luxury hardware |
| Quality tailoring | 20pts | Well-structured, quality stitching, designer touches |
| Standard tailored | 15pts | Basic tailoring, clean lines, simple details |
| Mid-construction | 10pts | Standard construction, basic hardware |
| Simple/Basic | 5pts | Basic tee, simple construction, minimal details |

**3. LENGTH/COVERAGE SCORE (0-20 points):**
| Length/Style | Points | Description |
|--------------|--------|-------------|
| Floor-length formal | 20pts | Gowns, formal √°o d√†i, bridal trains |
| Maxi/Long formal | 18pts | Maxi dresses, long elegant pieces |
| Midi formal | 15pts | Midi dresses with formal styling |
| Knee-length structured | 12pts | Pencil skirts, structured knee dresses |
| Above-knee casual | 8pts | Casual dresses, skater skirts |
| Mini/Shorts | 5pts | Mini dresses, shorts, casual mini |

**4. COLOR/PATTERN SCORE (0-20 points):**
| Color/Pattern | Points | Examples |
|---------------|--------|----------|
| Metallics/Luxury | 20pts | Gold, silver, rose gold, metallic fabrics |
| Rich jewel tones | 18pts | Emerald, sapphire, ruby red, amethyst |
| Elegant neutrals | 15pts | Champagne, ivory, taupe, camel, navy |
| Soft pastels | 12pts | Blush pink, powder blue, lavender, mint |
| Classic solids | 10pts | Black, white, gray, beige basics |
| Bold prints | 8pts | Vibrant patterns, graphic prints |
| Basic colors | 5pts | Basic tee colors, simple solids |

**SCORING FORMULA:**
```
Total Score = Fabric (0-30) + Design (0-30) + Length (0-20) + Color (0-20)
Maximum possible: 100 points
```

**TIER ASSIGNMENT:**
- **80-100 points** ‚Üí ‚≠ê‚≠ê‚≠ê TIER 1 Premium locations
- **50-79 points** ‚Üí ‚≠ê‚≠ê TIER 2 Upscale locations
- **0-49 points** ‚Üí ‚≠ê TIER 3 Accessible locations

üì¶ ENVIRONMENT + STYLING PACKAGES (6 TYPES)

- **Color Grade:** Warm nostalgic tones, soft highlights, cultural authenticity
- **Best for:** √Åo d√†i (all types), traditional Vietnamese wear, cultural fashion, heritage pieces

- **Props:** Coffee cup, minimalist furniture, succulents/plants, books, laptop, modern art
- **Styling:** Contemporary jewelry (geometric, minimal), natural/textured hair, modern heels or designer sneakers, structured bag
- **Camera:** Clean composition with negative space, 50mm f/2.8, modern aesthetic, geometric lines
- **Color Grade:** Clean bright tones, slight desaturation, contemporary feel
- **Best for:** Office wear, cocktail dresses, √°o d√†i c√°ch t√¢n, casual premium, smart casual

**PACKAGE D - URBAN CASUAL (Tier 2-3, 40-70pts):**

**PACKAGE E - NATURAL LIFESTYLE (Tier 3, 20-50pts):**

**PACKAGE F - BEACH/RESORT (Tier 2-3, for specific products):**

- **Color Grade:** Vibrant blues and greens, warm sun tones, tropical saturated

üîÑ AUTO-SELECTION WORKFLOW
================================================

**STEP-BY-STEP PROCESS:**

```
INPUT: Product from outfit reference image
  ‚Üì
STEP 1: ANALYZE PRODUCT ATTRIBUTES
  ‚Üí Identify fabric type
  ‚Üí Assess design complexity
  ‚Üí Determine length/silhouette
  ‚Üí Evaluate color/pattern
  ‚Üì
STEP 2: CALCULATE SCORES
  ‚Üí Fabric Score (0-30)
  ‚Üí Design Score (0-30)
  ‚Üí Length Score (0-20)
  ‚Üí Color Score (0-20)
  ‚Üí TOTAL (0-100)
  ‚Üì
STEP 3: DETERMINE TIER
  ‚Üí 80-100pts = Tier 1 (Premium)
  ‚Üí 50-79pts = Tier 2 (Upscale)
  ‚Üí 0-49pts = Tier 3 (Accessible)
  ‚Üì
STEP 4: IDENTIFY PRODUCT TYPE/OCCASION
  ‚Üí Bridal/Evening? ‚Üí Package A or B
  ‚Üí √Åo d√†i? ‚Üí Package B (Heritage)
  ‚Üí Office/Casual Premium? ‚Üí Package C
  ‚Üí Streetwear/Casual? ‚Üí Package D
  ‚Üí Loungewear/Home? ‚Üí Package E
  ‚Üí Swimwear/Resort? ‚Üí Package F
  ‚Üì
STEP 5: SELECT MATCHING PACKAGE
  ‚Üí Match tier + occasion
  ‚Üí Get environment + lighting + props + styling
  ‚Üì
STEP 6: CHOOSE SPECIFIC LOCATION
  ‚Üí From package's tier category
  ‚Üí Check against blocklist
  ‚Üí Ensure diversity (no recent repeats)
  ‚Üí Prefer suggested locations if provided
  ‚Üì
STEP 7: APPLY PACKAGE SPECIFICATIONS
  ‚Üí Set lighting setup from package
  ‚Üí Add appropriate props
  ‚Üí Define styling details
  ‚Üí Set camera specs
  ‚Üì
OUTPUT: Complete environment setup ready for generation
  ‚Üí environment: "[specific location with details]"
  ‚Üí lighting: "[package lighting specs]"
  ‚Üí props: "[package props list]"
  ‚Üí styling: "[package styling guide]"
  ‚Üí camera: "[package camera settings]"
```

================================================
‚öôÔ∏è IMPLEMENTATION NOTES
================================================

**FOR AI SYSTEM:**
1. **Always calculate scores** before selecting environment
2. **Document scoring** in metadata for transparency
3. **Match package to both tier AND occasion** for best results
4. **Check blocklist** before finalizing location choice
5. **Apply all package elements** (environment + lighting + props + styling + camera)
6. **NO PEOPLE IN BACKGROUND (ABSOLUTE RULE):**
   - **CRITICAL:** Prompts MUST specify "empty location, no people in background, isolated setting"
   - ‚ùå **NEVER:** Busy cafes, crowded streets, populated parks, shopping areas, public spaces with people
   - ‚ùå **NEVER describe:** "people walking in distance", "crowd in background", "passersby", "other people"
   - ‚úÖ **ALWAYS:** Private indoor (studio, home, hotel suite), isolated outdoor (empty beach, quiet garden), off-peak deserted locations
   - ‚úÖ **ALWAYS add to prompt:** "Empty location with no other people visible, isolated setting, private space"
   - **Why:** Background people = Distraction, AI generation errors (wrong faces), privacy issues, unprofessional look

7. **Environment-Outfit Compatibility (CRITICAL):**
   - **Match cultural/formality level:** Casual clothes ‚â† Heritage/Temple locations
   - **WRONG Pairings (Fix immediately):**
     - ‚ùå S∆∞·ªùn x√°m/Tank top/Casual tee + Temple/Pagoda/Heritage site ‚Üí Use home/studio instead
     - ‚ùå Loungewear/Pajamas + Luxury hotel lobby ‚Üí Use bedroom instead
     - ‚ùå Streetwear/Denim + Formal restaurant ‚Üí Use urban street/cafe instead
     - ‚ùå Bikini/Swimwear + City indoor ‚Üí Use beach/pool instead
   - **CORRECT Pairings:**
     - ‚úÖ √Åo d√†i traditional + Temple/Heritage site
     - ‚úÖ Evening gown + Luxury hotel/Restaurant
     - ‚úÖ Casual wear + Home/Cafe/Studio
     - ‚úÖ Streetwear + Urban street/Industrial space
     - ‚úÖ Swimwear + Beach/Pool
   - **Rule:** If outfit tier ‚â† location tier ‚Üí Choose matching tier location
     - Tier 3 outfit (casual basic) ‚Üí Tier 3 location (home, studio, simple cafe)
     - Tier 1 outfit (formal, √°o d√†i) ‚Üí Tier 1 location (heritage, luxury)

================================================
üó∫Ô∏è REAL LOCATIONS ONLY (MANDATORY)
================================================

**GOLDEN RULE:** Every environment MUST be a REAL location verifiable on Google Maps.

**‚ö†Ô∏è WHY CRITICAL:**
- Authentic real locations = Photorealistic results
- Specific places = Better AI understanding of architecture, lighting, atmosphere
- Verifiable addresses = Consistent quality control

**‚ùå NEVER USE (Generic/Fictional):**
- "Luxury hotel lobby" (too vague)
- "Beautiful temple" (no specific location)
- "Modern cafe" (no name or address)
- "Beach resort" (fictional)
- "Traditional Vietnamese house" (generic)
- "5-star restaurant" (no venue name)

**‚úÖ ALWAYS USE (Real & Specific):**
- "Park Hyatt Saigon - Grand Lobby, 2 Lam Son Square, District 1"
- "VƒÉn Mi·∫øu Qu·ªëc T·ª≠ Gi√°m (Temple of Literature) - Main courtyard, Dong Da District, Hanoi"
- "The Workshop Coffee - 27 Nguyen Hue, District 1, Ho Chi Minh City"
- "InterContinental Danang Sun Peninsula Resort - Beachfront area, Son Tra Peninsula"
- "Ph·ªë c·ªï H·ªôi An - Tran Phu Street yellow wall area, Hoi An Ancient Town"

**LOCATION NAMING REQUIREMENTS:**

All locations MUST include:
1. **Exact venue name** (official name, can check on Google Maps)
2. **Specific area/room** within venue (lobby, courtyard, rooftop, etc.)
3. **Address or landmark** reference (street, district, or famous landmark)

**FORMAT TEMPLATE:**
```

```

üé¨ CINEMATIC SCENE TRANSITION RULES (GH√âP N·ªêI M∆Ø·ª¢T M√Ä)

**3. QUY T·∫ÆC CAMERA (CAMERA CONTINUITY):**

- Dolly shot: gi·ªØ nguy√™n h∆∞·ªõng v√† t·ªëc ƒë·ªô

**4. QUY T·∫ÆC √ÅNH S√ÅNG (LIGHTING CONTINUITY):**

üéµ BEAT-SYNC CHOREOGRAPHY (TIKTOK AUTO-CUT READY)

ƒê·ªÉ video ph√π h·ª£p v·ªõi nh·∫°c TikTok auto-cut, m·ªçi pose + motion PH·∫¢I ƒë∆∞·ª£c thi·∫øt k·∫ø theo nh·ªãp.

**üéØ BEAT-SYNC PHILOSOPHY:**

‚Üí Pose/motion PH·∫¢I c√≥ "impact moment" kh·ªõp v·ªõi beat.

**üìä BPM CATEGORIES & MOTION TIMING (∆ØU TI√äN SMOOTH FLOW):**
| BPM Range | Nh·ªãp | Beat Interval | Motion Style | Pacing |
|-----------|------|---------------|--------------|--------|
| 60-80 | Slow | 1.0s-0.75s | Slow, dreamy, cinematic | ∆ØU TI√äN - Elegant |
| 80-100 | Mid-tempo | 0.75s-0.6s | Graceful, flowing | ∆ØU TI√äN - Natural |
| 100-120 | Moderate | 0.6s-0.5s | Smooth transitions | OK - Balanced |
| 120-140 | Mid-fast | 0.5s-0.43s | Gentle accents | H·∫°n ch·∫ø |
| 140+ | Fast | <0.43s | KH√îNG KHUY·∫æN KH√çCH | Tr√°nh |

**üé¨ BEAT-MATCHED ACTIONS (SMOOTH FLOW PRIORITY):**
| Beat Type | Action | Camera Response |
|-----------|--------|-----------------|
| Downbeat (1) | GENTLE ACCENT - subtle pose shift | Smooth zoom / Slow pan |
| Upbeat (2,4) | MICRO-MOTION - hair flow, fabric sway | Gradual tilt |
| Accent | SOFT PAUSE - graceful hold | Slow push-in |
| Build-up | CONTINUOUS FLOW - smooth motion | Gentle orbit |
| Transition | FLOWING SHIFT - natural movement | Dolly in/out |

**üï∫ GRACEFUL MOTION LIBRARY (Cho Smooth Flow):**

**ELEGANT TRANSITIONS (cho accent moments):**

- "Gentle hair touch, fingers gliding through strands"
- "Soft fabric adjustment, hands tracing hemline"
- "Fluid turn 45¬∞, maintaining eye contact"
- "Elegant shoulder roll, neck stretching gently"

**SMOOTH FLOWS (cho continuous motion):**

- "Shoulder roll freeze, fabric draping"
- "Weight shift left, subtle head tilt"

**MICRO-MOTIONS (between beats):**

- "Fabric rippling subtly"
- "Fingers trailing along fabric"
- "Slight sway, weight transfer"
- "Breath movement, chest rise"

**üéº SCENE STRUCTURE BY MUSIC SECTION:**

**INTRO (00s-08s) - Scene 1:**
- BPM: Match song intro (usually slower build)
- Pose: Reveal pose ‚Üí Build-up motion
- Camera: Slow push-in or orbit
- Beat sync: Every 2-4 beats = subtle motion

**VERSE (08s-16s) - Scene 2:**
- BPM: Steady rhythm
- Pose: Flowing sequences, storytelling
- Camera: Smooth tracking or pan
- Beat sync: Every beat = micro-motion

**BRIDGE (16s-24s) - Scene 3:**
- BPM: Same as previous (consistent)
- Pose: Graceful continuation, natural flow
- Camera: Same smooth pacing, gentle orbit
- Beat sync: Gentle accents, continuous movement

**FINALE (24s-32s) - Scene 4:**
- BPM: Same as previous scenes (consistent pacing)
- Pose: Signature final pose, elegant and memorable
- Camera: Smooth continuation, no sudden speed change
- Beat sync: Natural flow, matching previous scenes' rhythm

   - Scene k·∫øt th√∫c v·ªõi pose "ready to move"

================================================
üìπ TIKTOK AUTOCUT CAMERA OPTIMIZATION
================================================

**üéØ PURPOSE:** Structure camera movements to enable TikTok autocut feature to automatically detect 4-6 cut points for dynamic multi-scene editing.

**HOW TIKTOK AUTOCUT WORKS:**
- Detects visual differences between frames (zoom changes, angle shifts)
- Identifies stable frames as natural cut points
- Auto-segments video into multiple clips based on scene changes

**OPTIMIZATION STRATEGY:**
- Use distinct zoom levels per scene (Wide ‚Üí Medium ‚Üí Close ‚Üí Wide)
- Hold stable frames at scene boundaries (1-2s) for clear cut detection
- Create 4 scenes = 3-4 potential auto-cut opportunities

---

### **ZOOM LEVEL DEFINITIONS (Veo 3.1 Compatible)**

**üìê Wide Shot (Full Body + Environment):**
- Framing: Head to toe, full outfit visible
- Environment: 40% frame showing location context
- Use for: Establishing shots, full look reveals, scene endings
- Example: "Wide shot showing full body from head to heels, Park Hyatt lobby visible in background"

**üìê Medium Shot (Waist Up + Some Environment):**
- Framing: Waist/hips to head
- Environment: 20% frame showing location hints
- Use for: Mid-scene transitions, outfit upper detail
- Example: "Medium shot from waist up, showing √°o d√†i top detail and face expression"

**üìê Close-Up (Chest/Face + Minimal Environment):**
- Framing: Chest/shoulders to top of head
- Environment: Minimal (10% frame)
- Use for: Product detail focus, fabric texture, facial expression
- Example: "Close-up on chest area showing embroidery detail, face partially visible"

**üìê Extreme Close (Product Detail Only):**
- Framing: Product feature filling frame
- Environment: None or blurred background
- Use for: Fabric texture, pattern detail, craftsmanship showcase
- Example: "Extreme close-up on silk fabric showing sheen and floral pattern"

---

### **PAUSE-HOLD-MOVE PATTERN (CRITICAL for Autocut)**

**Structure for each 8-second scene:**

```
‚îú‚îÄ 0-1s: HOLD START (Stable frame - autocut detection point)
‚îÇ         Camera stationary, clear composition
‚îÇ         
‚îú‚îÄ 1-7s: SMOOTH ZOOM (Transition execution)
‚îÇ         Slow zoom in/out over 6 seconds
‚îÇ         Veo 3.1 optimal speed: smooth, cinematic
‚îÇ         
‚îî‚îÄ 7-8s: HOLD END (Stable frame - next cut point)
          Camera settled, clear end composition
```

**WHY THIS WORKS:**
- Start hold (1s) = Clear beginning frame ‚Üí TikTok detects scene start
- Smooth zoom (6s) = Beautiful cinematic movement
- End hold (1s) = Clear ending frame ‚Üí TikTok detects cut point
- Next scene starts with different zoom level ‚Üí Visual contrast ‚Üí Autocut triggers

---

### **CAMERA PATTERN 1: Progressive Zoom In (4-6 Cuts)**

**Best for:** Product showcase, detail revelation, fashion editorial

**Scene 1 (0-8s): Wide ‚Üí Medium**
```json
{
  "cameraMotion": "Slow zoom in from wide to medium shot over 6 seconds",
  "startFrame": "Wide shot - full body visible, environment context clear",
  "endFrame": "Medium shot - waist up, focus shifting to upper outfit",
  "timing": {
    "holdStart": "0-1s static wide",
    "zoomExecution": "1-7s smooth zoom in",
    "holdEnd": "7-8s static medium"
  },
  "autoCutPoint": "8s - stable medium shot frame"
}
```

**Scene 2 (8-16s): Medium ‚Üí Close**
```json
{
  "cameraMotion": "Continue zoom in from medium to close-up over 6 seconds",
  "startFrame": "Medium shot - picking up from Scene 1 end",
  "endFrame": "Close-up - chest/product detail visible",
  "timing": {
    "holdStart": "8-9s static medium",
    "zoomExecution": "9-15s smooth zoom in",
    "holdEnd": "15-16s static close"
  },
  "autoCutPoint": "16s - stable close-up frame"
}
```

**Scene 3 (16-24s): Close ‚Üí Extreme Close**
```json
{
  "cameraMotion": "Final zoom in to extreme close on product detail",
  "startFrame": "Close-up from Scene 2",
  "endFrame": "Extreme close - fabric texture/pattern fills frame",
  "timing": {
    "holdStart": "16-17s static close",
    "zoomExecution": "17-23s slow zoom to extreme",
    "holdEnd": "23-24s static extreme"
  },
  "autoCutPoint": "24s - product detail frame"
}
```

**Scene 4 (24-32s): Zoom Out Reveal**
```json
{
  "cameraMotion": "Pull out from extreme close to wide reveal",
  "startFrame": "Extreme close from Scene 3",
  "endFrame": "Wide shot - full look reveal, complete outfit visible",
  "timing": {
    "holdStart": "24-25s static extreme",
    "zoomExecution": "25-31s smooth zoom out",
    "holdEnd": "31-32s static wide (final reveal)"
  },
  "autoCutPoint": "32s - final wide frame"
}
```

**Autocut Result:** 4 clear cut points at 8s, 16s, 24s, 32s

---

### **CAMERA PATTERN 2: In-Out Rhythm (5-6 Cuts)**

**Best for:** Dynamic fashion, movement showcase, energetic vibe

**Scene 1 (0-8s): Wide ‚Üí Close (Fast Zoom In)**
- Start: Wide full body
- Zoom: Quick transition to close-up over 6s
- End: Close product focus
- **Big visual change = Strong autocut trigger**

**Scene 2 (8-16s): Close ‚Üí Wide (Zoom Out)**
- Start: Close from Scene 1
- Zoom: Pull out to wide over 6s
- End: Wide full reveal
- **Zoom direction reversal = Clear cut point**

**Scene 3 (16-24s): Wide ‚Üí Medium**
- Start: Wide from Scene 2
- Zoom: Gentle zoom to medium
- End: Medium waist-up
- **Subtle zoom = Softer transition**

**Scene 4 (24-32s): Medium ‚Üí Close (Final Focus)**
- Start: Medium
- Zoom: Final zoom to close detail
- End: Close product highlight
- **Ending close-up = Strong finish**

**Autocut Result:** 5 cut points (more dynamic pacing)

---

### **CAMERA PATTERN 3: Detail Focus (Product Storytelling)**

**Best for:** Luxury items, craftsmanship showcase, high-end fashion

**Scene 1 (0-8s): Wide Establishing Shot**
```
Camera: Wide static shot with subtle slow orbit (10¬∞ rotation over 8s)
Purpose: Establish environment and full look
Hold: 1s start, 1s end
Autocut: Clear wide frame at 8s
```

**Scene 2 (8-16s): Zoom to Upper Body**
```
Camera: Zoom from wide to medium, focus on upper outfit
Purpose: Highlight top design, fabric, collar detail
Hold: 1s start, 1s end
Autocut: Medium shot frame at 16s
```

**Scene 3 (16-24s): Extreme Close ‚Äì Product Detail**
```
Camera: Zoom to extreme close on key feature (embroidery, texture, button)
Purpose: Showcase craftsmanship, quality, unique details
Hold: 2s on extreme close (allow detail appreciation)
Autocut: Product detail frame at 24s
```

**Scene 4 (24-32s): Pull Back to Full Reveal**
```
Camera: Smooth zoom out from extreme to wide
Purpose: Show complete look in context after detail exploration
Hold: 1s wide final frame
Autocut: Final reveal at 32s
```

**Autocut Result:** 4 cuts with strong visual storytelling

---

### **IMPLEMENTATION GUIDELINES**

**‚úÖ DO (Autocut-Friendly):**
- Hold stable for 1-2s at scene start/end
- Use distinctly different zoom levels between scenes
- Maintain smooth zoom speed (6s transitions)
- End each scene with clear, well-composed frame

**‚ùå DON'T (Breaks Autocut):**
- Continuous zoom across all scenes (no cut points)
- Same zoom level throughout (no visual variation)
- Fast snap zooms (< 3s) - too jerky for Veo 3.1
- No stable frames (camera always moving)

---

    }

### **TIKTOK AUTOCUT EXPECTED RESULTS**

**With Optimization (This System):**
- 32s video ‚Üí 4 scenes
- TikTok autocut detects: **4-6 cut points**
- Auto-generated segments: 4-6 dynamic clips
- Edit-ready for music sync, beat matching

**Without Optimization:**
- 32s video ‚Üí Continuous smooth motion
- TikTok autocut detects: **1-2 cuts** (minimal)
- Limited auto-editing capability

**Benefits:**
‚úÖ Maximum editing flexibility
‚úÖ Dynamic multi-angle feel
‚úÖ Professional pacing automatically
‚úÖ Beat-sync ready (if music added)
‚úÖ Higher engagement (varied visual rhythm)

**üé¨ QUICK START TEMPLATE:**

Use Progressive Zoom In (Pattern 1) as default for most fashion videos:
- Scene 1: Wide ‚Üí Medium (full look to upper body)
- Scene 2: Medium ‚Üí Close (detail focus)
- Scene 3: Close ‚Üí Extreme (product showcase)
- Scene 4: Extreme ‚Üí Wide (final reveal)

**Result:** Clean 4-scene structure, maximum autocut compatibility ‚ú®
